steal_popularity_from_fiscal_liberals = {
	#Western conservatives
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.1
	}
	#Western liberals
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^2 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.2
	}
	#Neutral conservatives
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^14 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 14 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.14
	}
	#Neutral libertarians
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^16 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.16
	}
}

				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.2
	}
	#Western socialism
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^3 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 3 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.3
	}
	#Emerging communism
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^4 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.4
	}
	#Emerging left wing radical
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^5 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.5
	}
	#Neutral libertarians
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^16 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.16
	}
	#Neutral greens
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^17 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 17 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.17
	}
	#Neutral socialists
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^18 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 18 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.18
	}
	#Neutral communism
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^19 > 0.01 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 19 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = attract_voters_pos.19
	}
}

##Marco Outlook
# arg_popularity (temp var): The amount of popularity you want to add to the outlook. #
add_ruling_outlook_popularity = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = arg_popularity
		}
	}
	else_if = { limit = { has_government = communism }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = arg_popularity
		}
	}
	else_if = { limit = { has_government = fascism }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = arg_popularity
		}
	}
	else_if = { limit = { has_government = neutrality }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = arg_popularity
		}
	}
	else_if = { limit = { has_government = nationalist }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = arg_popularity
		}
	}
	recalculate_party = yes
}

# Adjust Election Threshold
# set_temp_variable = { threshold_change = +- }
modify_election_threshold = {
	add_to_variable = { election_threshold = threshold_change }
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_election_threshold_tt
	clamp_variable = {
		var = election_threshold
		min = 0
		max = 0.10
	}
	update_dirty_subideology = yes
}

set_party_index_to_ruling_party = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_array = {
				array = ruling_party
				value = 0
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = western_technocrat
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_array = {
				array = ruling_party
				value = 0
			}
			has_country_leader_with_trait = western_technocrat
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = gov_coalition_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^v > biggest_party_in_coalition_popularity }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { biggest_party_in_coalition_popularity = party_pop_array^v }
				set_temp_variable = { biggest_party_in_coalition = v }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = biggest_party_in_coalition }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 1 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 2 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 3 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 4 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 5 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 6 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 7 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 8 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 9 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 10 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 11 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 11 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 12 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 12 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 13 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 13 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 14 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 14 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 15 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 16 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 17 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 17 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 18 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 18 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 19 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 19 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 20 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 21 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 22 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 23 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
	}
}

# Add Relative Party Popularity:
#
# This scripted effect adds (or substracts) relative party popularity. How to use:
#
# 2022/04/30 - Added a additional parameter Z to allow you to increase the outlook within the script
#
# set_temp_variable = { party_index = X } #Index of party to be changed 0-23
# set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = Y } #How much party popularity is changed, must be in decimals so 2% is 0.02
# set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = Z } #OPTIONAL PARAMETER -- Must be in decimals so 2% is 0.02
# add_relative_party_popularity = yes
#
#NOTE! The temp variable names must be the same as above!
add_relative_party_popularity = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = TT_ADD_RELATIVE_PARTY_POPULARITY
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_index = 0 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 1 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 2 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 3 }
			}
		}

		# If you have the optional parameter. First ADD the new outlook percentage.
		if = { limit = { has_variable = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
		}
		else = {
			#Set the old remainder Outlook based on non-boosted parties
			set_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_popularity@democratic }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Add X% to party popularity, this is the popularity we want the party to retain!
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
			#Set the new remainder Outlook
			set_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_popularity@democratic }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Scale all non-boosted parties
			divide_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = old_outlook_remainder }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = party_pop_array
				value = v
				index = i

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { i = party_index } }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { i = 0 }
							check_variable = { i = 1 }
							check_variable = { i = 2 }
							check_variable = { i = 3 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^i = outlook_remainder }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 5 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 6 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 7 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 8 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 9 }
			}
		}
		# If you have the optional parameter. First ADD the new outlook percentage.
		if = { limit = { has_variable = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
		}
		else = {
			#Set the old remainder Outlook based on non-boosted parties
			set_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_popularity@communism }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Add X% to party popularity, this is the popularity we want the party to retain!
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
			#Set the new remainder Outlook
			set_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_popularity@communism }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Scale all non-boosted parties
			divide_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = old_outlook_remainder }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = party_pop_array
				value = v
				index = i

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { i = party_index } }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { i = 4 }
							check_variable = { i = 5 }
							check_variable = { i = 6 }
							check_variable = { i = 7 }
							check_variable = { i = 8 }
							check_variable = { i = 9 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^i = outlook_remainder }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_index = 10 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 11 }
			}
		}

		# If you have the optional parameter. First ADD the new outlook percentage.
		if = { limit = { has_variable = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
		}
		else = {
			#Set the old remainder Outlook based on non-boosted parties
			set_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_popularity@fascism }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Add X% to party popularity, this is the popularity we want the party to retain!
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
			#Set the new remainder Outlook
			set_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_popularity@fascism }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Scale all non-boosted parties
			divide_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = old_outlook_remainder }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = party_pop_array
				value = v
				index = i

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { i = party_index } }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { i = 10 }
							check_variable = { i = 11 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^i = outlook_remainder }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_index = 12 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 13 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 14 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 15 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 16 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 17 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 18 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 19 }
			}
		}

		# If you have the optional parameter. First ADD the new outlook percentage.
		if = { limit = { has_variable = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
		}
		else = {
			#Set the old remainder Outlook based on non-boosted parties
			set_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_popularity@neutrality }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Add X% to party popularity, this is the popularity we want the party to retain!
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
			#Set the new remainder Outlook
			set_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_popularity@neutrality }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Scale all non-boosted parties
			divide_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = old_outlook_remainder }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = party_pop_array
				value = v
				index = i

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { i = party_index } }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { i = 12 }
							check_variable = { i = 13 }
							check_variable = { i = 14 }
							check_variable = { i = 15 }
							check_variable = { i = 16 }
							check_variable = { i = 17 }
							check_variable = { i = 18 }
							check_variable = { i = 19 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^i = outlook_remainder }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_index = 20 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 21 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 22 }
				check_variable = { party_index = 23 }
			}
		}

		# If you have the optional parameter. First ADD the new outlook percentage.
		if = { limit = { has_variable = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = temp_outlook_increase }
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
		}
		else = {
			#Set the old remainder Outlook based on non-boosted parties
			set_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_popularity@nationalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { old_outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Add X% to party popularity, this is the popularity we want the party to retain!
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^party_index = party_popularity_increase }
			#Set the new remainder Outlook
			set_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_popularity@nationalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = party_pop_array^party_index }
			#Scale all non-boosted parties
			divide_temp_variable = { outlook_remainder = old_outlook_remainder }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = party_pop_array
				value = v
				index = i

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { i = party_index } }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { i = 20 }
							check_variable = { i = 21 }
							check_variable = { i = 22 }
							check_variable = { i = 23 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^i = outlook_remainder }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	recalculate_party = yes
}

effect_puppet_match_ruling_party_to_overlord = {		#Used in target scope
	#Remove old parties from power
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array

	#Western
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = democratic has_elections = yes } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = democratic has_elections = no } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = no }
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 0 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
		set_country_flag = set_Western_Autocracy
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 1 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
		set_country_flag = set_conservatism
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 2 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
		set_country_flag = set_liberalism
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 3 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
		set_country_flag = set_socialism
	}

	#Emerging
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = communism has_elections = yes } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = communism has_elections = no } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 4 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
		set_country_flag = set_Communist-State
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 5 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
		set_country_flag = set_anarchist_communism
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 6 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
		set_country_flag = set_Conservative
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 7 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
		set_country_flag = set_Autocracy
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 8 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 8 }
		set_country_flag = set_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 9 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 9 }
		set_country_flag = set_Vilayat_e_Faqih
	}

	#Salafism
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = fascism has_elections = yes } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = fascism has_elections = no } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 10 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 10 }
		set_country_flag = set_Kingdom
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 11 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 11 }
		set_country_flag = set_Caliphate
	}

	#Non-aligned
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = neutrality has_elections = yes } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = neutrality has_elections = no } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 12 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 12 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 13 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_Autocracy
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 14 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_conservatism
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 15 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
		set_country_flag = set_oligarchism
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 16 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_Libertarian
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 17 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_green
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 18 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
		set_country_flag = set_neutral_Social
	}

		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
		set_country_flag = set_Neutral_Communism
	}

	#Nationalist
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = nationalist has_elections = yes } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = nationalist elections_allowed = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_government = nationalist has_elections = no } }

	}

		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
		set_country_flag = set_Nat_Autocracy
	}
	if = { limit = { FROM = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 23 } } }
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
		set_country_flag = set_Monarchist
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ruling_party
		value = v
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^v = 0.50 }
	}
	update_party_name = yes
	set_leader = yes
}

set_temp_variable_to_ruling_party = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 1 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 2 } }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { array = ruling_party value = 3 } }

#### New Coalition stuff ####
startup_politics = {
	set_failsafe_values = yes #adds needed values if missing
	add_up_party_totals = yes
	set_party_positions = yes
	setup_election_threshold = yes #adds election_threshold if not set
	store_election_values = yes #add to election array
	update_majority_threshold = yes
	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
	update_party_name = yes
	reset_coalition_ideas = yes
	find_two_highest_parties = yes
	if = { limit = { is_debug = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: startup_politics executed"
	}
}

start_politics_input = {
	clear_array = party_pop_array
	clear_array = party_pop_elect_array
	clear_array = pos_array
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array

	resize_array = { array = party_pop_array size = 24 }
	resize_array = { array = party_pop_elect_array size = 24 value = -1 }
	resize_array = { array = pos_array size = 24 }
	update_dirty_subideology = yes
}

recalculate_party = {
	hidden_effect = {
		add_up_party_totals = yes
		set_party_positions = yes
		update_government_coalition_strength = yes
		update_dirty_subideology = yes
	}
}

# stores the info of popularities. modified version of store_election_values = yes
hold_elections = {
	# Technocrat Trait
	if = { limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = western_technocrat }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = 0 } #technocrats don't participate in elections
	}
	add_up_party_totals = yes
	set_party_positions = yes
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = partyall_banned } }
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = party_pop_array^num
			value = v
			if = {
				limit = {
					# normal popularity entry is over threshold
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^v > election_threshold }
				}
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = party_pop_array^v }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		# Should set the main election value and ignore the election threshold
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ruling_party
			set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^i = party_pop_array^i }
		}
	}
	calculate_banned_parties = yes
	update_majority_threshold = yes
	find_two_highest_parties = yes
	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
}

recalculate_party_strength = {
	add_up_party_totals = yes
	set_party_positions = yes
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = partyall_banned } }
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = party_pop_array^num
			value = v
			if = {
				limit = {
					# normal popularity entry is over threshold
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^v > election_threshold }
				}
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = party_pop_array^v }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		# Should set the main election value and ignore the election threshold
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ruling_party
			set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^i = party_pop_array^i }
		}
	}
	update_majority_threshold = yes
}

add_up_party_totals = {

	set_variable = { pop_total_democratic = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_communism = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_fascism = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = 0 }

	#Outlook popularity based on party popularities (removed the unnecessary loop)
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_democratic = party_pop_array^0 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_democratic = party_pop_array^1 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_democratic = party_pop_array^2 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_democratic = party_pop_array^3 }

	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^4 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^5 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^6 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^7 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^8 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_communism = party_pop_array^9 }

	add_to_variable = { pop_total_fascism = party_pop_array^10 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_fascism = party_pop_array^11 }

	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^12 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^13 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^14 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^15 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^16 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^17 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^18 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = party_pop_array^19 }

	add_to_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = party_pop_array^20 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = party_pop_array^21 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = party_pop_array^22 }
	add_to_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = party_pop_array^23 }

	#Scale party popularity totals to match actual Outlook popularity
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = current_id
		multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = 1000 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id < 4 }
			}
			divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = pop_total_democratic }
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = party_popularity@democratic }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 3 }
				check_variable = { current_id < 10 }
			}
			divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = pop_total_communism }
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = party_popularity@communism }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { current_id = 10 }
					check_variable = { current_id = 11 }
				}
			}
			divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = pop_total_fascism }
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = party_popularity@fascism }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 11 }
				check_variable = { current_id < 20 }
			}
			divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = pop_total_neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = party_popularity@neutrality }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 19 }
			}
			divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = pop_total_nationalist }
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = party_popularity@nationalist }
		}
		divide_variable = { party_pop_array^current_id = 1000 }
		clamp_variable = { var = party_pop_array^current_id min = 0 max = 1 }
	}

	#Make sure there are no Outlooks with popularity without any party popularities
	#Make 1% the limit, as smaller than that isn't visible on the chart
	if = {
		limit = {
			democratic > 0.01
			check_variable = { pop_total_democratic < 0.01 }
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^1 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^3 = 0.01 } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			communism > 0.01
			check_variable = { pop_total_communism < 0.01 }
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^4 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^5 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^7 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_idea = shia } } add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^8 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_idea = shia } } add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^9 = 0.01 } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			fascism > 0.01
			check_variable = { pop_total_fascism < 0.01 }
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^10 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^11 = 0.01 } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			neutrality > 0.01
			check_variable = { pop_total_neutrality < 0.01 }
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^12 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^13 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^14 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^15 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^16 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^17 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^18 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^19 = 0.01 } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			nationalist > 0.01
			check_variable = { pop_total_nationalist < 0.01 }
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^20 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^21 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^22 = 0.01 } }
			10 = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^23 = 0.01 } }
		}
	}

}

set_party_positions = {
	resize_temp_array = {
		array = party_pop_array_temp
		size = 24
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = pos_array^num
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = party_pop_array
			value = max
			index = max_index
		}
		set_variable = { pos_array^v = max_index }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^max_index = -1 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_pop_array_temp^max_index = max }
	}
	clear_array = party_pop_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = party_pop_array_temp
		add_to_array = { party_pop_array = v  }
	}
	clear_temp_array = party_pop_array_temp
}

find_two_highest_parties = {
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = max_1_tmp
		index = max_index_1_tmp
	}
	set_variable = { max_index_1 = max_index_1_tmp }
	set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^max_index_1 = -1 }
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = max_2_tmp
		index = max_index_2_tmp
	}
	set_variable = { max_index_2 = max_index_2_tmp }
	set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^max_index_1 = max_1_tmp }
}

update_party_name = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { ruling_party^num > 0 }
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = [OUTLOOK]
					name = [SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME]
					long_name = [SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME]
				}
			}
			OUTLOOK = "[meta_ideology_names]"
			SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME = "[show_ruling_party]"
		}
	}
}

# Function: gov_pop_calculation
# Purpose: The gov pop calculation is to calculate the penalty from your government popularity swinging
# from -100% to 100% of their current popularity
# How-to Adjust: Adjust the penalty by changing line 1904 from 0.002 to 0.005
gov_pop_calculation = {
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = government_popularity_modifier } } }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = government_popularity_modifier }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { add_t = government_coalition_differential }
	multiply_temp_variable = { add_t = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = add_t max = 100 min = -100 }

	subtract_from_temp_variable = { add_t = 0 }

	set_variable = { gov_pop_stability_factor = add_t }
	set_variable = { gov_pop_political_power_factor = add_t }

	multiply_variable = { gov_pop_stability_factor = 0.002 }
	multiply_variable = { gov_pop_political_power_factor = 0.002 }

	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

set_coalition_drift = {
	#reset coalition counts
	set_variable = { coalition_fascism = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_nationalist = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_communism = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_neutrality = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_democratic = 0 }
	clear_coalition_count_ideas = yes

	#Each coalition partner popularity gets added to their own Outlook
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = gov_coalition_array^num
		value = v
		set_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^gov_coalition_array^v } #pop of current element
		set_temp_variable = { current_id = gov_coalition_array^v } #ID of current element
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id < 4 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { coalition_democratic = sum }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 3 }
				check_variable = { current_id < 10 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { coalition_communism = sum }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { current_id = 10 }
					check_variable = { current_id = 11 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { coalition_fascism = sum }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 11 }
				check_variable = { current_id < 20 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { coalition_neutrality = sum }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_id > 19 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { coalition_nationalist = sum }
		}
	}

	#Don't get bonuses to ruling Outlook
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = democratic }
		set_variable = { coalition_democratic = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_government = communism }
		set_variable = { coalition_communism = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_government = fascism }
		set_variable = { coalition_fascism = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_government = neutrality }
		set_variable = { coalition_neutrality = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_government = nationalist }
		set_variable = { coalition_nationalist = 0 }
	}

	reset_democratic_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_neutrality_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_communism_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_nationalist_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_fascism_coalition_ideas = yes
}

update_government_coalition_strength = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_debug = yes }
		log = "[This.GetName] update_government_coalition_strength"
	}
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = gov_coalition_array
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_array^v }
	}
	set_variable = { government_coalition_strength = sum }

	#strength of ruling_party is separate
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ruling_party
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_array^v }
	}
	add_to_variable = { government_coalition_strength = sum }

	### Now setup the election strength ###
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = gov_coalition_array
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^v }
	}
	set_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect = sum }

	#strength of ruling_party is separate
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ruling_party
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^v }
	}
	add_to_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect = sum }

	#find the differentials
	set_variable = { government_coalition_differential = government_coalition_strength }
	subtract_from_variable = { government_coalition_differential = government_coalition_strength_elect }
	gov_pop_calculation = yes
	set_coalition_drift = yes
}

refund_government_coalition = {
	set_temp_variable = { sum_factor = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = v
		set_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^gov_coalition_array^v } #pop of current element
		set_temp_variable = { current_id = gov_coalition_array^v } #ID of current element
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				pol_distance_matrix_[NUM] = yes
			}
			NUM = "[?current_id|.0]"
		}
		set_temp_variable = { pol_dist_temp = pol_distance_current }
		multiply_temp_variable = { sum = pol_distance_current }
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum_factor = sum }
	}
	set_variable = { pp_cost_to_invite = sum_factor }
	multiply_variable = { pp_cost_to_invite = 1500 } #75%
	add_political_power = pp_cost_to_invite
	log = "[GetDateText]: [THIS.GetName]: DEBUG CODE 69420: PP Refund: [?pp_cost_to_invite], Pop of Current Element: [?sum], Current ID: [?current_id], Pol Distance Current: [?pol_distance_current], Sum Factor: [?sum_factor]"
}

store_election_values = {

	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = v
		if = {
			limit = {
				#true if no specific value has already been set
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					#normal popularity entry is over threshold
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^v > election_threshold }
				}
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = party_pop_array^v }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = -1 }
				}
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	calculate_banned_parties = yes
}

#only on startup
setup_election_threshold = {
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = election_threshold } }
		set_variable = { election_threshold = 0.05 } #5% used as default
	}
}

#only needed for elections
update_majority_threshold = {
		set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			add_to_temp_variable = { sum = v }
		}
		set_variable = { majority_threshold = sum }
		divide_variable = { majority_threshold = 2 }
}

campaign_spending_initial = {
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count < 3 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.6 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 3 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.68 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 4 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.76 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 5 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.80 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 6 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.84 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 7 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.88 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 8 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.92 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 9 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.96 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 10 } }
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 0.96 }
			}
			50 = {
				set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.04 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 11 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.04 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 12 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.08 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 13 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.12 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 14 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.16 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count = 15 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.2 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { campaign_funding_count > 15 } }
		set_variable = { ads_budget_effect = 1.24 }
	}
}

# AI create coalition
AI_setup_government = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_debug = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: AI started setup government [?political_power]"
	}
	# hold_elections = yes #add values to election array etc
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array

	set_temp_variable = { majority_threshold_1 = majority_threshold } #need one that does not include biggest party
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_threshold_1 = party_pop_elect_array^max_index_1 }

	set_temp_variable = { majority_threshold_2 = majority_threshold } #need one that does not include second biggest party
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_threshold_2 = party_pop_elect_array^max_index_2 }

	make_affinity_arrays = yes
	reduce_affinity_array_party_1 = yes
	reduce_affinity_array_party_2 = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			#coalition 1 is prefered - lowest
			check_variable = {
				var = cost1
				value = cost2
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			index = i1
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^i1 > 0 }
				}
				add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = i1 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { cost1 > cost2 } #coalition 2 is prefered - lowest
		}
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = max_index_2 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			index = i2
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^i2 > 0 }
				}
				add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = i2 }
			}
		}
	}

	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
	set_coalition_drift = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = ITA
		}
		reforme_expectance_government_change_update = yes
		calculate_abandon_coalition_threshold = yes
		remove_gov_crisis_ai_flags	= yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			#leader has subideology_trait = ruling party
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_technocrat
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_conservatism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_liberalism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_socialism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_anarchist_communism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Conservative
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Vilayat_e_Faqih
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Caliphate
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_conservatism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_oligarchism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Libertarian
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_green
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_neutral_Social
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Populism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Fascism
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#switch to ruling
		hidden_effect = {
			set_ruling_leader = yes
			set_leader = yes
		}
	}
	# Logs the AI Setup_government
	if = {
		limit = { is_debug = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: AI finished setup government [?political_power]"
	}
}

make_affinity_arrays = {
	resize_temp_array = {
		array = party_1_affinity_array
		size = party_pop_array^num
	}
	resize_temp_array = {
		array = party_2_affinity_array
		size = party_pop_array^num
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = v
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { max_index_1 = v }
					check_variable = { max_index_2 = v }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v > 0 }
				}
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						party_1_pol_distance_[NUM] = yes
					}
					NUM = "[?v|.0]"
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^v = pol_distance_current }
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						party_2_pol_distance_[NUM] = yes
					}
					NUM = "[?v|.0]"
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^v = pol_distance_current }
			}
		}
	}
}


reduce_affinity_array_party_1 = {

	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = a1
		break = break_1
		set_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_1 = 0 }

		#current temp coalition1 strength
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			value = b1
			index = e1
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^e1 > 0 }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_1 = b1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { sum_coalition_1 > majority_threshold_1 }
			}
			find_highest_in_array = {
				array = party_1_affinity_array
				value = max1
				index = max1_index
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_1 = party_pop_elect_array^max1_index }
			set_temp_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^max1_index = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { sum_coalition_1 < majority_threshold_1 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^max1_index = max1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_1 = party_pop_elect_array^max1_index }
				set_temp_variable = { break_1 = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	#find total cost1
	set_temp_variable = { cost1 = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = d1
		index = g1
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_1_affinity_array^g1 > 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { cost1_element = party_1_affinity_array^g1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cost1_element = d1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { cost1 = cost1_element }
		}
	}
}

reduce_affinity_array_party_2 = {

	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = a2
		break = break_2
		set_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_2 = 0 }

		#current temp coalition2 strength
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			value = b2
			index = e2
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^e2 > 0 }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_2 = b2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { sum_coalition_2 > majority_threshold_2 }
			}
			find_highest_in_array = {
				array = party_2_affinity_array
				value = max2
				index = max2_index
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_2 = party_pop_elect_array^max2_index }
			set_temp_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^max2_index = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { sum_coalition_2 < majority_threshold_2 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^max2_index = max2 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { sum_coalition_2 = party_pop_elect_array^max2_index }
				set_temp_variable = { break_2 = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	#find total cost2
	set_temp_variable = { cost2 = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = d2
		index = g2
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_2_affinity_array^g2 > 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { cost2_element = party_2_affinity_array^g2 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cost2_element = d2 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { cost2 = cost2_element }
		}
	}
}

		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } } #anarchist_communism
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } } #Autocracy
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.7 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } #Conservative
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.7 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } } #Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } } #Vilayat_e_Faqih
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } } #Kingdom
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.7 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } } #Caliphate
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 } } #Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } } #Neutral_Autocracy
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.5 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } } #Neutral_conservatism
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.9 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } } #oligarchism
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.8 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } } #Neutral_Libertarian
		set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } } #Neutral_green
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } } #neutral_Social
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } } #Neutral_Communism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.9 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } #Nat_Populism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } } #Nat_Fascism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } } #Nat_Autocracy
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.3 }
	}
}

# Add Coalition Member
# set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = 0-23 } -- Required
add_coalition_members_effect = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = add_coalition_members_effect_TT
	add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = add_col_one }
	hidden_effect = {
		update_government_coalition_strength = yes
		set_coalition_drift = yes
	}
}

# Remove Coalition Member
# set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = 0-23 }
remove_coalition_members_effect = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = remove_coalition_members_effect_TT
	remove_from_array = { gov_coalition_array = remove_col_one }
	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
	set_coalition_drift = yes
}

# Change Party Command
# set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 0-23 }
# set_temp_variable = { col_one = 0 - 23 }  -- Optional
# set_temp_variable = { col_two = 0 - 23 }  -- Optional
# set_temp_variable = { col_three = 0 - 23 }  -- Optional
# set_temp_variable = { change_leader_temp = 0-1 } -- Optional
change_ruling_party_effect = {
	# Do Not Retire Section
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { change_leader_temp = 1 } }
		set_country_flag = do_not_retire
	}

	# Clears the Parameters
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array

	# Rul Party Addition
	set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = rul_party_temp }
	custom_effect_tooltip = ruling_party_changed_tt
	add_to_array = { ruling_party = add_col_one }

	# Coalition Array Parameters
	if = { limit = { has_variable = col_one }
		set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = col_one }
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_coalition_members_effect_TT
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = add_col_one }
	}
	if = { limit = { has_variable = col_two }
		set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = col_two }
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_coalition_members_effect_TT
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = add_col_one }
	}
	if = { limit = { has_variable = col_three }
		set_temp_variable = { add_col_one = col_three }
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_coalition_members_effect_TT
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = add_col_one }
	}

	hidden_effect = {
		update_government_coalition_strength = yes
		update_party_name = yes
		set_coalition_drift = yes
		set_ruling_leader = yes
		set_leader = yes
	}
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { change_leader_temp = 1 } }
		clr_country_flag = do_not_retire
	}
}

# update_dirty_subideology
# Purpose: updates the subideology dirty variable to ensure the UI is up-to-date
update_dirty_subideology = {
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { global.subideologies_view_main < 100000 } }
		add_to_variable = { global.subideologies_view_main = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { global.subideologies_view_main = 0 }
	}
}

# ban_party_scripted_call
# Parameters: party_index - 1-24
# Purpose: Bans the provided party index from elections
ban_party_scripted_call = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_country_flag = party[v]_banned
		}
		v = "[?party_index|.0]"
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { party_index = -1 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = ban_party_effect_tt
	update_dirty_subideology = yes
}

# unban_party_scripted_call
# Parameters: party_index - 1-24
# Purpose: Allows the provided party index for elections
unban_party_scripted_call = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			clr_country_flag = party[v]_banned
		}
		v = "[?party_index|.0]"
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { party_index = -1 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = unban_party_effect_tt
	update_dirty_subideology = yes
}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = party1_banned }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { pp_cost = 10 }
		set_country_flag = party1_banned
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
